  <script type="text/javascript">
   function getCookie(cname) {
  var name = cname + '=';
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
      c = c.substring(1);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
      return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    }
  }
  return '';
}

function handleInterstitial() {
  var ref = document.referrer;
  document.cookie="ns=1";
  //In incognito mode, first time there is no cookie and user won't get interstitial, so setting a cookie
  // so that it doesn't return first time in incognito

  if (
    window.nsShowMaxCount < 1 ||
    window.isPrime ||
    window.location.host.match(/toispadev/) ||
    (ref.match(/defaultinterstitial/) && getCookie('nsIstial')) ||
    document.cookie === '' ||
    /bot|googlebot|crawler|spider|robot|crawling/i.test(navigator.userAgent)
  ) {
    //toiprops.cookie.remove('nsIstial');
    document.cookie = 'nsIstial=; expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 UTC; domain=.indiatimes.com';
    return true;
  }

  var goToInterstitialPage = function() {
    var queryParams = window.location.search;
    window.location.replace(
      'https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/' + (window.location.pathname === '/us'? 'defaultinterstitial_int_us': 'defaultinterstitial' ) + '.cms' +
        queryParams
    );
  };

  var nsShownCount = parseInt(getCookie('nsIstial_Cook'), 10) || 0;

  // if use has been in the same session and refreshed the page more than 10 times
  // reset the flags
  if (nsShownCount > 10) {
    document.cookie = 'nsIstial_Cook=null';
    nsShownCount = 0;
  }

  if (nsShownCount < window.nsShowMaxCount) {
    if (
      !(
        window.location.href.indexOf('order_id') > -1 &&
        localStorage.getItem('toi_subscription')
      )
    ) {
      nsShownCount += 1;
      document.cookie = 'nsIstial_Cook=' + nsShownCount;
      goToInterstitialPage();
    }
  }
  else{
    nsShownCount += 1;
    document.cookie = 'nsIstial_Cook=' + nsShownCount;
  }

  return;
}

if (
  window.nsShowMaxCount > 0 &&
  !window.location.href.match(/TOI_browsernotification/)
) {
  handleInterstitial();
}

          <div class="NL-VD _2QHcl">
           <h2 class="_36fs8">
            <a class="Yjv6u" data-newga="EntertainmentSection_Actions#EntertainmentClick-Featured/Grid3/Movie Reviews_HeadingClick" frmappuse="1" href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/entertainment/hindi/movie-reviews">
             Movie Reviews
            </a>
           </h2>
          </div>
          <div>
           <div class="_1bad5">
            <a data-newga="EntertainmentSection_Actions#EntertainmentClick-Featured/Grid3/0//entertainment/hindi/movie-reviews/sandeep-aur-pinky-faraar/movie-review/81579122.cms" frmappuse="1" href="https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/entertainment/hindi/movie-reviews/sandeep-aur-pinky-faraar/movie-review/81579122.cms">
             <img alt="" imgsize="23456" msid="" offsetvertical="0" placeholdermsid="" placeholdersrc="" resizemode="4" title="" type="thumb"/>
             <div class="LazyLoad" style="height:1px">
             </div>
             <div class="_3h8TN">
              <h2>
               Sandeep Aur Pinky Faraar
              </h2>
              <p>
               Sandeep and Pinky Faraar is one of those neo-noir films that set out with a promise to engage, entertain and educate by slowly unraveling its layered subtext. But with its preposterous execution and frustratingly slow pace, its the audience who might want to escape, much before Sandeep and Pinky.
              </p>
              <div class="_2EPGY">
               <span>
                Critic Rating
               </span>
               <span class="_1QuRC">
                2.5
               </span>
              </div>
             </div>
            </a>
           </div>

             <img alt="" imgsize="23456" msid="" offsetvertical="0" placeholdermsid="" placeholdersrc="" resizemode="4" title="" type="thumb"/>
             <div class="LazyLoad" style="height:1px">
             </div>
             <div class="_3h8TN">
              <h2>
               Mumbai Saga
              </h2>

               If you like gritty gangster dramas packed with brawn, blood and bullets then Mumbai Saga could be worth a watch.
              </p>
